)@@G@@@^@@@Q LET M=51+OPTS:H*17     @]@@@Q LET X=0    @]@@@Q LET L=0    @]@@@QGG
)@@G@@ LET N=0    @]@@@Q DO FOREVER @#@@@Q GET SKEL(EOF=EOF)@#@@@Q LET T=IOBUFGH
)@@G@@[0]:H1@]@@@Q LET I=0    @D@@@Q IF T='*IF' OR T='*IN' OR T='*CO' OR T='*DGI

)@@G@@ MAX # OF BYTES TO PRINT@ @@@Q LET K=K-132 @ AMOUNT OVER 132@ @@@Q IF K<GR
)@@G@@=0 THEN @ NO OVERFLOW   @A@T@Q WRITE TEXT V,N,<IOBUF:0,NWORDS-1>  @ @@@TGS
)@@G@@ WRITE TEXT V,N,<IOBUF:0,J>   @[@@@Q ELSE @ @@@Q LET K=(K+5)/6 @ # EXTRAGT
)@@G@@ WORDS@]@@@T LET J=J-K  @ @T@Q WRITE TEXT V,N,<IOBUF:0,J-K> @ @@@T WRITEGU
)@@G@@ TEXT V,N,<IOBUF:0,J>   @ @S@Q WRITE EXTRA <IOBUF:0,J-K+1,J>@ @T@S WRITEGV
)@@G@@ EXTRA <IOBUF:J-K+1,J>  @A@@@T WRITE EXTRA <IOBUF:J+1,NWORDS-1>   @[@@@QGW
)@@G@@END IF@C@T@QEXTRA: FORMAT '--CONTINUED IMAGE-->',<K>F6,*    @C@@@TEXTRA:GX
)@@G@@ FORMAT '--CONTINUED IMAGE-->',<K>F6,*    @C@T@QTEXT: FORMAT Z2,' ',D5,'GY
)@@G@@: ',X(V*2),<NWORDS>F6,* @C@@@TTEXT: FORMAT Z2,' ',D5,': ',X(V*2),<J+1>F6GZ
